347→func (s *Service) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n   348→\tinterval := s.cfg.SSOSettingsReloadInterval\n   349→\tif interval == 0 {\n   350→\t\treturn nil\n   351→\t}\n   352→\n   353→\tticker 371→\tsettingsList, err := s.List(ctx)\n   372→\tif err != nil {\n   373→\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to fetch SSO Settings for all providers\", \"err\", err)\n   374→\t\treturn\n   375→\t}\n   376→\n {\n   387→\t\t\ts.metrics.reloadFailures.WithLabelValues(provider).Inc()\n   388→\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to reload SSO Settings\", \"provider\", provider, \"err\", err)\n   389→\t\t\tcontinue\n   390→\t\t}\n   391→\t}\n   392→}\n   393→\n   394→// mergeSSOSettings merges the settings from the database with the system settings\n   395→// Required because it is possible that the user has configured some of the settings (current Advanced OAuth settings)\n   396→// and the rest of the settings have to be loaded from the system settings\n   397→func (s *Service) mergeSSOSettings(dbSettings, systemSettings *models.SSOSettings) *models.SSOSettings {\n   398→\tif dbSettings == nil {\n   399→\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"No SSO Settings found in the database, using system settings\")\n   400→\t\treturn systemSettings\n   401→\t}\n   402→\n   403→\ts.logger.Debug(\"Merging SSO Settings\", \"dbSettings\", removeSecrets(dbSettings.Settings), \"systemSettings\", 414→}\n   415→\n   416→func (s *Service) decryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   417→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(settings)\n   418→\n   419→\tfor _, 424→\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to parse secret value, it is not a string\", \"key\", k)\n   425→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n   426→\t\t\t\t}\n   427→\n   428→\t\t\t\tdecoded, err := base64.RawStdEncoding.DecodeString(strValue)\n   429→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   430→\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"Failed to decode secret string\", \"err\", err, \"value\")\n 467→\treturn result\n   468→}\n   469→\n   470→// getConfigMaps returns a list of maps that may contain secrets\n   471→func getConfigMaps(settings map[string]any) []map[string]any {\n   472→\t// 488→\n   489→// mergeSettings merges two maps in a way that the values from the first map are preserved\n   490→// and the values from the second map are added only if they don't exist in the first map\n   491→// or if they contain empty URLs.\n   492→func mergeSettings(storedSettings, systemSettings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n   493→\tsettings := make(map[string]any)\n   494→\n   495→\tfor k, v := range storedSettings {\n   496→\t\tsettings[k] = v\n   497→\t}\n   498→\n   499→\tfor k, v := range systemSettings {\n   500→\t\tif _, ok := settings[k]; !ok {\n   501→\t\t\tif an empty string with their value\n   506→\t\t\t// from the system settings. This fixes an issue with empty auth_url, api_url and token_url\n   507→\t\t\t// from the DB not being replaced with their values defined in the system settings for\n   508→\t\t\t// the Google provider.\n   509→\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t}\n   512→\n   513→\treturn settings\n   514→}\n   515→\n   516→// isMergingAllowed returns true if the field provided can be merged from the system settings.\n   517→// It won't allow SAML fields that are part of a group of settings to be merged from system settings\n   518→// because the DB settings already contain one valid setting from each group.\n   519→func isMergingAllowed(fieldName string) bool {\n   520→\tforbiddenMergePatterns := []string{\"certificate\", \"private_key\", \"idp_metadata\"}\n   521→\n   522→\tfor 528→}\n   529→\n   530→// mergeSecrets returns a new map with the current value for secrets that have not been updated\n   531→func mergeSecrets(settings map[string]any, storedSettings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   532→\tsettingsWithSecrets := deepCopyMap(settings)\n   533→\tnewConfigs := getConfigMaps(settingsWithSecrets)\n   534→\tstoredConfigs := getConfigMaps(storedSettings)\n   535→\n   536→\tfor i, config := range newConfigs {\n   537→\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n   538→\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) {\n   539→\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n   540→\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   541→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n   542→\t\t\t\t}\n   543→\n   544→\t\t\t\tif !isNewSecretValue(strValue) && len(storedConfigs) > i {\n   545→\t\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = storedConfigs[i][k] // use the currently stored value\n   546→\t\t\t\t}\n   547→\t\t\t}\n   548→\t\t}\n   549→\t}\n   550→\n   551→\treturn settingsWithSecrets, nil\n   552→}\n   553→\n   554→func overrideMaps(maps ...map[string]any) map[string]any {\n   555→\tresult := make(map[string]any)\n   556→\tfor _, m := range maps {\n   557→\t\tfor k, v := range m {\n   558→\t\t\tresult[k] = v\n   559→\t\t}\n   560→\t}\n   561→\treturn result\n   562→}\n   563→\n   564→// IsSecretField returns true if the SSO settings field provided is a secret\n   565→func IsSecretField(fieldName string) bool {\n   566→\tsecretFieldPatterns := []string{\"secret\", \"private\", \"certificate\", \"password\", \"client_key\"}\n   567→\n   568→\tfor _, v := range secretFieldPatterns {\n   569→\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n   570→\t\t\treturn true\n   571→\t\t}\n   572→\t}\n   573→\treturn false\n   574→}\n   575→\n   576→func isURL(fieldName string) bool {\n   577→\treturn strings.HasSuffix(fieldName, \"_url\")\n   578→}\n   579→\n   580→func isEmptyString(val any) bool {\n   581→\t_, ok := val.(string)\n   582→\treturn ok && val == \"\"\n   583→}\n   584→\n   585→func isNewSecretValue(value string) bool {\n   586→\treturn value != setting.RedactedPassword\n   587→}\n   588→\n   589→func deepCopyMap(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n   590→\tnewSettings := make(map[string]any)\n   591→\n   592→\tfor key, value := range settings {\n   593→\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n   594→\t\tcase map[string]any:\n   595→\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopyMap(v)\n   596→\t\tcase []any:\n   597→\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopySlice(v)\n   598→\t\tdefault:\n   599→\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = value\n   600→\t\t}\n   601→\t}\n   602→\n   603→\treturn newSettings\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→func deepCopySlice(s []any) []any {\n   607→\tnewSlice := make([]any, len(s))\n   608→\n   609→\tfor i, value := range s {\n   610→\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n   611→\t\tcase map[string]any:\n   612→\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = deepCopyMap(v)\n   613→\t\tcase []any:\n   614→\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = deepCopySlice(v)\n   615→\t\tdefault:\n   616→\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = value\n   617→\t\t}\n   618→\t}\n   619→\n   620→\treturn newSlice\n   621→}\n   622→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider the system settings. This fixes an issue with empty auth_url, api_url and token_url\n\t\t\t// from the DB not being replaced with their values defined in the system settings for\n\t\t\t// the Google
